 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Important Additional Information Regarding Proxy Solicitation </B>Exxon Mobil Corporation (&#147;ExxonMobil&#148;) has
filed a definitive proxy statement and form of associated BLUE proxy card with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) in connection with the solicitation of proxies for ExxonMobil&#146;s 2021 Annual Meeting (the
&#147;Proxy Statement&#148;). ExxonMobil, its directors and certain of its executive officers will be participants in the solicitation of proxies from shareholders in respect of the 2021 Annual Meeting. Information regarding the names of
ExxonMobil&#146;s directors and executive officers and their respective interests in ExxonMobil by security holdings or otherwise is set forth in the Proxy Statement. To the extent holdings of such participants in ExxonMobil&#146;s securities are
not reported, or have changed since the amounts described, in the Proxy Statement, such changes have been reflected on Initial Statements of Beneficial Ownership on Form 3 or Statements of Change in Ownership on Form 4 filed with the SEC. Details
concerning the nominees of ExxonMobil&#146;s Board of Directors for election at the 2021 Annual Meeting are included in the Proxy Statement. BEFORE MAKING ANY VOTING DECISION, INVESTORS AND SHAREHOLDERS OF THE COMPANY ARE URGED TO READ ALL RELEVANT
DOCUMENTS FILED WITH OR FURNISHED TO THE SEC, INCLUDING THE COMPANY&#146;S DEFINITIVE PROXY STATEMENT AND ANY SUPPLEMENTS THERETO AND ACCOMPANYING BLUE PROXY CARD, BECAUSE THEY CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION. Investors and shareholders can obtain a
copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant documents filed by ExxonMobil free of charge from the SEC&#146;s website, www.sec.gov. ExxonMobil&#146;s shareholders can also obtain, without charge, a copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant
filed documents by directing a request by mail to ExxonMobil Shareholder Services at 5959 Las Colinas Boulevard, Irving, Texas, 75039-2298 or at shareholderrelations@exxonmobil.com or from the investor relations section of ExxonMobil&#146;s website,
www.exxonmobil.com/investor. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g175478g0419211322401.jpg" ALT="LOGO">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">P&amp;GA&#146;s corporate advertising team has launched digital ad campaigns in the U.S. for policy,
financial and opinion leader audiences on a targeted basis on premium news sites, social media and streaming audio/podcasts. Ad formats include online videos, animated and static banners, audio spots and social media sponsorships. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Policy and financial audience advertisements highlight ExxonMobil&#146;s emissions reduction plans and new Low Carbon Solutions business&nbsp;(<U>click
here</U> to view), while opinion leader audience advertisements feature ExxonMobil&#146;s research, expertise and partnerships (<U>available here</U>).</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Placements include prominent news outlets such as Financial Times, The Economist, Forbes, The Hill, New York Times, The Atlantic, Bloomberg, Washington Post,
ABC News and CNN, as well as streaming services such as Spotify and podcasts from NPR and Wall Street Journal.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If you would like more information about
these campaigns, please contact Adrienne Handford or Jillian Fleming.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">[Embed video:
https://wdrv.it/present-project-detail/assetId/103155794/token/7f562bae6/presentationId/16820245] </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The ads, which are playing across digital and social platforms in the United States, feature our emissions reduction plans, our new Low Carbon Solutions
business, and partnerships with universities and government labs to research breakthrough technologies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Watch the ads below. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Important Additional Information Regarding Proxy Solicitation</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Exxon Mobil Corporation (&#147;ExxonMobil&#148;) has filed a definitive proxy statement and form of associated BLUE proxy card with the U.S. Securities and
Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) in connection with the solicitation of proxies for ExxonMobil&#146;s 2021 Annual Meeting (the &#147;Proxy Statement&#148;). ExxonMobil, its directors and certain of its executive officers will be
participants in the solicitation of proxies from shareholders in respect of the 2021 Annual Meeting. Information regarding the names of ExxonMobil&#146;s directors and executive officers and their respective interests in ExxonMobil by security
holdings or otherwise is set forth in the Proxy Statement. To the extent holdings of such participants in ExxonMobil&#146;s securities are not reported, or have changed since the amounts described, in the Proxy Statement, such changes have been
reflected on Initial Statements of Beneficial Ownership on Form 3 or Statements of Change in Ownership on Form 4 filed with the SEC. Details concerning the nominees of ExxonMobil&#146;s Board of Directors for election at the 2021 Annual Meeting are
included in the Proxy Statement. BEFORE MAKING ANY VOTING DECISION, INVESTORS AND SHAREHOLDERS OF THE COMPANY ARE URGED TO READ ALL RELEVANT DOCUMENTS FILED WITH OR FURNISHED TO THE SEC, INCLUDING THE COMPANY&#146;S DEFINITIVE PROXY STATEMENT AND
ANY SUPPLEMENTS THERETO AND ACCOMPANYING BLUE PROXY CARD, BECAUSE THEY CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION. Investors and shareholders can obtain a copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant documents filed by ExxonMobil free of charge from the
SEC&#146;s website,<B>&nbsp;www.sec.gov</B>. ExxonMobil&#146;s shareholders can also obtain, without charge, a copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant filed documents by directing a request by mail to ExxonMobil Shareholder Services at 5959
Las Colinas Boulevard, Irving, Texas, 75039-2298 or at<B>&nbsp;shareholderrelations@exxonmobil.com</B>&nbsp;or from the investor relations section of ExxonMobil&#146;s website,<B>&nbsp;www.exxonmobil.com/investor</B>. </P>
